Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of which there is a manner such that you make three or four cauteries, aligning according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cautery as we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand too much on the cautery, and let the patient often lie on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another manner of cautery is that you heat the cautery with two nerves, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the heart which is near the mouse, or where the stitches of the patient come to the left side, and let the elevations on which you lift the heart be according to the shape of the heart, according to the length of the body, and the cautery be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After pouring out the two flaming wicks until their cores are pierced from the other side, then remove the cautery, and thus it will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see, cautery the entire cautery to three wicks.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has rotted for a long time, and this must be done differently from the previous wounds.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery is not suitable for dropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure it according to the methods we have said in divisions, and your cure does not help much, then you must make four cauteries around the wound, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one at the anus;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauteries be close to the edge of the wick.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After let the cautery open to drain putridity long enough, and do not delay the treatment of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and the healing would be hastened, and the two intentions would be combined with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly should be the claw-like one that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and for the back, it should be olive-shaped, according to what was mentioned before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in those who are dropsical and are full of yellow bile, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the foot between the auricular and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and hold your hand with the fire cautery without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, otherwise it would burn yellowish, and let the cauterizes be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	after make on each leg two cauteries at the tip of the cuticular;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauteries be long, one above the knee in front and the other below, between the legs;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries on for a long time without curing, until the ache subsides;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the treatment of other wounds as we have said.
de la menoison	of the reduction
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	when the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, since the retaining and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be treated by methods of wound care;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and with much virtue, make the great cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken about earlier or stomach cautery, in the cautery circle;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four small cauteries between the lips for each small cautery, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moistures and the patient suffering, make him undergo the fire cautery on the armpit, and two cauterizations on each leg, and two small cauterizations on the stomach below the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are internal or external, and are old and are large cold and moist humors腐化, and are treated as we have said in the sections, and it does not improve, then make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the spine of the back, that one just above the iliac crest a little bit at a time in a triangular manner, and one cautery below the lip two digits.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cooled and the meat does not cook, and one sees the fat swelling, then heat the fat on the stomach as was said before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen for the entire cautery.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain long enough.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment, let the limb heal until it is sane.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the carbuncle which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cauterize the ulcer, heat the cautery until it seems red-hot, and then apply it completely burning over the ulcer being treated.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand remain there until the cautery reaches the base of the vein, so that it heals.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much ulceration, cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the application of ointments until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery over the navel, it will have greater aid.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure incision or opening, which we will describe in its place, comes a disease that cannot be healed except by fire cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is a fistula and it is infected with decayed pus and moisture, you should probe the entire length of the wound with a sharp probe, and ensure that you know the full length of the wound.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	heat the cautery until it seems red-hot, and apply it to the fistula according to the quantity that the pus has entered, and reapply the cautery until the corrupt flesh is burned, one time, or two or three times, according to the quantity needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the nerves that are nearby, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestine, beware of these areas, and do not perform this outside the fatty tissue, and think that it is not harmful.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after the treatment of the eye until it is healed, and if the eyes are inflamed, and the materials have been removed for a long time, then know that the eyes are completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the materials have not been removed, know that the eye is inflamed, and the bone is corrupted.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and in the manner as one of those that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes with strong winds, and does not take hold of a woman, then you must cauterize the sides of the ribs on both sides with the claw cautery as we have already mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will do more great aid.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make a fire cautery in the part below the bladder, where the hairs begin at the base of the penis, both on the right and on the left, and let each cautery be as long as one inch.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make the cautery below the spine, or where you may need it;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cauteries be of the shape as previously described.
de la marris	of the gallbladder
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the matrix is cold and moist, and does not allow conception as a result, and the flowers are corrupted and their termination delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to make three cauteries on the cheek, as we have said for the bladder cautery, and two behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauteries be on the arm, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When slimy moistures descend to the socket of the hip, and for this reason it moves out of its place; the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and find the location from which the slimy moisture departs, and it is necessary to cauterize the patient on the socket of the hip with one cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the location within the socket as it turns, so that the socket lies within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cauteries are such as those from which one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if such cauteries are not present to you, make three cauteries of olive oil great, and let the cauteries be as perfect as all the quires.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue the treatment until he is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the socket of the hip, and it is due to cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we said in the division, and the treatment is ineffective, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the patient of the large humors with foul pills or other good pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you perform the fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together with burning medicines, and the fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	The fire cautery is carried out in many ways, of which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the socket of the hip with three triangular cauteries in this form, and do them to good depth and large, with an space the width of a thumb between each cautery, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes the cauterization is done in the middle on the head of the hip, for which there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, cauterize with the cautery of the circle that we have already mentioned before regarding the dislocation of the hip.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a manner that the circle contains the entire hip, and all the points of the knee be arsed.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way we treat sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations there or where the patient says the pain is, and one cauterization above the ankle on the left side slightly.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauterizations be with a lancet, and sear the thickness of the knee.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two points of the foot or near it, cauterize where he feels the pain with three or four cauterizations called "poins.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if the task is, let him do more;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is from below the knee to the thigh, then make a fire cautery with a cutellar or circular cautery, and take great care in all your cauteries that you do not leave the cautery on too long so as to burn the nerves and the large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient any greater harm or contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed a cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it on too long until the leg was completely swollen, and the foot as well, and all the feet were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a belly purge from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two parts together, perform a cautery in one and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said about the cautery for the hip, as follows: make the iron such that it is at the head as thick as a nail's head, or a bit less, and let it be jagged, and let it be between the fingers and be from one finger's breadth to another of the quantity of a nut's length;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the splints be over two parts, and be also like nuts, and have one iron hand well made.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is completely red and emit sparks, and then place it on the socket of the injured hip, and turn it towards the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let the cautery be applied once the heat is reduced and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply a poultice of butter, and keep the wound open long enough.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the ointment treatment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use this cautery little because of the fear of its sight, and we see few who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and wherever this is well cauterized, who can bear it, and let it be where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery for burning medicine is made by preparing an instrument of tongs in which the margin of the mouthpiece descends, and it should be made of tin or iron on one side long, and at the height of two nails, and each should have the size of a thumb.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and be open at the top and above, and join together according to this form.
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the hip box on the patient lying on their side with the healthy side up, and pressing your hand firmly on the hip box;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	after pouring between the two circles of the hot awe for a little while heated on fire, and let it remain one hour or so, and allow the patient to endure the heat and the burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	Because there is also a bite from a fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the bite has passed, remove your hand with the instrument and lift the awed side gently, and leave it for three days, and apply butter until the blackness from the scalding is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it remain for three days that the putrefaction draws out;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last aid after the treatment with ointments until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or to the leg, apply the tool that hurts awe according to what you did for the hip equally;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the way of the hot awe, and I have written about it in the treatise on the rectification of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or there be the small hole pierced such that the point of a razor may be able to enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place in it another that is well weighted, and put on alkali and wax and mild awe, as much as there are two on top of the powders as you will have well impressed with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until the wax and lead descend in the awe. Then take all that awe, and throw it on wax and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will become very wet and is administered in degrees of medicinal works and other limb cauteries.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes great work like fire, and with other medicines where one cauterizes well the hip as with tinese and honey of anacard and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment where a noble was cured of the pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and the loincache, and says that no other treatment was done, and he was cured at one time when this treatment was performed, and he bathed as he teaches hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And it is said in such a manner that you take fresh and dry litharge green, and grind it much with a little grease, and apply it to the hip and thigh and leg where the pain resides, and mix it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and he leaves it for three hours and by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed, and make him go to bed, and the pain will all go away and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such a cautery with these medicines if it is not after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides said that when the sciatic vein is cauteryed with sheep's fat, it greatly helps;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery must be made in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and grease it with old oil, and apply it to the depression between the big toe and the other toe called the fossicle.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry sheep's fat, hold it over fire until it becomes hot coals, and place it on the wool, and let it remain until it is cool;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do this again, and continue in this manner until you think by sense that it has reached the hip, and the pain is ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this manner of cautery is called "sheep cautery.
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain from the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back from falling or percussion or due to too great an evacuation or similar to matter expanded cold, none of these circumstances calls for cautery, though it may be necessary for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It must be that the patient is free of foul pills or other similar things, and upon their back, where the pain resides, three lines marked with enche, in each line five cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cauteries should be done according to the cautery called "poins";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauteries at the medium clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this illness comes upon small children, and the signs of the beginning are that their throat is narrow when they arise, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find at the last spine of the back and in us the appearance that comes on the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and find it needs to be treated, cauterize it with the circular fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	That the cauterization for each part of the spine increases accordingly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, cauterize between the spines with a painful fire cautery two or three lines wide, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the treatment of the limb until it is healed as we have said, and make sure you do not apply a fire cautery to swelling that is in the spasm of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	And when joint pains are due to moistures spread throughout each limb of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which they call "podagre" properly, and when it is from a cold cause and cannot be cured by applications of medicines, it is cured by cautery in such a manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make many cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cauteries be olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need to prick the sole of the foot, let the cautery be as large as what we call "point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come as far as the knees and other joints, and this happens often, then make cauteries on each knee III or IV in each part, for the entire cautery with olive oil:
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have need of more, do more, but not to keep your hand away for longer than until the coals of the fire are extinguished.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and the back, apply the cautery as we have said in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make pricks around the wrist two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains any pain in the fingers, make pricks at each joint and above the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come as far as the elbows or as far as the shoulders, cautery each part, and give good governance to the patient and prudent medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give it good governance and purge the humor, it will be healed by the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the syphax
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	And when rupture comes in veins, and the bulges descend to the groin and this is newly occurring, then it is necessary that when you see them incised, he not eat at all that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and when he uses things that alleviate the belly, so that the phlegm descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after placing it on its back between your hands, and instruct him to stretch its belly until the boils are healed, then reduce them with your fingers and mark a line under the break in the bone of the arm, and make sure the mark is similar to half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery coal that has the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	while it remains white and gives off scents.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	then reduce the boils to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the minister stretches his hand so that the boils do not return;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and tend well to the thighs of the patient, and place a cushion and a mat over the thighs, and another over the foot that gives pain to the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery on the mark on your hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach the bone the first time, repeat another time until you come to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and carefully ensure that the boil does not burst when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	and do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die from this, or other harms.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the fire cautery, your efforts amount to nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it must be that the cauteries for children are fine according to the measure of their size, and those for adults as large according to their measure.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, cure the skin around the butter cautery until the scalding is removed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the initial treatment with other ointments until it is healed, and let the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it must be that the poultices are applied for a long time, so that the boils do not come to a head when he goes into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, apply a well-made bandage, and keep it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, that he works little and guards against too great fullness from drinking and eating, and from too loud shouting;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this instruction, he is completely cured.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after the treatment to shave in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other organs and are known, and you see that they do not increase, then apply the fire cautery as many times as necessary according to their quantity, and let it burn for one-third of the time.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a fire cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but mark the midpoint of the wound and draw a line along its width above the rupture, and another below it, and run your hand through all the cautery points.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and more painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, due to falling or injury, and that pain lasts a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "poins," and the cauterizations should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is healed from the first cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if this name, recommence with another cautery on that one, because such custom is that it must change to the part nearest to it, so you must make the cauteries as long as the patient is healed.
de meselerie	by means of craftiness
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The diseases are sometimes aided once by the fire cautery with great help, and especially those diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Cannot you see the patient needs cautery, take care that the disease is at the beginning, and it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and neither spreads nor remains, and if you doubt that the corruption may spread throughout the patient, then you make five cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I place the cautery on the neck, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hairline;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and on the two horns, and the rear one on the scapula;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let your hand remain until the cautery reaches the bone, and until the bark is removed so that the vapors of the excess humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what is said before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the mixture is spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and if it is clearly effective, then you must cauterize with the cautery as we have said or chief, and the third on the spine of the neck, and six on the spine of the back, and one large one on the shoulder blade and another on the side, and two on the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two over the shins, and two over the tendons of the foot, one over each joint of the hands and feet, and over the depressions of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and take care of the nerves that are over the buttocks, so you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and once the fire cautery is done on the bone of the thigh, one more on the bone of the abdomen, and one more on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more fire cauteries you perform, the more aid you provide, and they profit from it;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the sick do not feel pain from the fire cautery as the healthy do, because their body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it must be that the cauteries are large and small according to the members and joints, according to those you will find in kinds of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the cure, apply a paste of flour and honey with other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and poultices, and it is not yet healed, then I make cauterizations on the limb according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be a little deeper in the thickness of the knee.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes the cauterization is done with a hot iron and on the back, at the end of the nerve that causes the limb to lose movement, and thus the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in any case, no one should intervene unless they know the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	of scabs
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is advanced, and medical remedies are of no use, then cauterize with a slightly hot cautery, according to the thickness of the keratin, until the whiteness is removed and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then treat with a cure of flour of vervain and lentils with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood from colen and blood from alondra, each in part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix all together, and wrap with a cloth, and apply to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the cauterization of the chancre
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the chancre begins and you see it stop, cauterize with a circle-shaped cautery around the entire circumference of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And the sage said that one should also cauterize at the center of the sore.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and in all ways it seems to me not good, for I fear that it may be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have had it happen this way more than once.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and more improper is that it be cauterized between, in the cautery called "circule," as we have said when discussing cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called "adubelati," and it delays death either due to its excess or because of the acidity of the patient when they are decrepit (that is, too old), and the patient has little blood, or due to the tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hasten its death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then the cauterization is done with many small cauteries pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	after he lets it be thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	Car she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierce through the entire cautery, heat the cautery as described here:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of the disease called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced through the heart, and let the cautery be such that the patient feels it on the other side in this manner so that the course of putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cure with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another manner of disease is called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than a corrosion of the member, for it eats away at the members just as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a patient who can bear the entire fire cauterization, then heat the cautery claws very small and large, according to what is appropriate for the part or where the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	after the cauterization from all sides until you have eradicated all the corruption, and nothing of it remains, that everything which is corrupt be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it be for three days, and place on the cauterized parts a sufferable dressing with oil until the burn marks from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the application of ointments producing flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy flesh does not arise, it is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, resume the fire cautery on that which is delayed from the corrupted parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this mixture has been cured with medicinal water instead of the fire cautery once.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but still, the fire cautery is of greater help. I have already mentioned the treatment with medicinal water in the division.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take the quantity you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of blisters that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times, at the feet due to fires, a disease arises which is called "clos" according to our understanding, and it is a large lump that hardens the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization for this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, the fire cauterization, and the hot aqueous cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is when you heat the cautery tip as if it were the shaft of a cinder-tooth (a type of implement), and it should be made of good iron to the size that it can hold a nail from all sides, and it should have thin edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	after heating it up on the nail, turn your hand all around the nail until it comes to the end of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it be thus for three days until it begins to rot with pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then apply a plaster of crushed wild mallows with salt, and leave the plaster on all through the night, and the nail will fall off and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then anoint the limb with healing ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they have been converted by fire on the body, and this happens often in hands and feet, then you must apply a hot water cautery to it.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in such a manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a needle of iron or a branch of willow, and place it on the nail and the althea, that is to say for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the needle so that it burns completely around, then put some hot awn on it, and hold your hand well, and press your hand turning it such that the edge of the needle comes to the base of the nail, and then find the hot awn deep path all the way to the base.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure for a while the burning from the hot awn for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it like this, and it will fall off completely with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Make one after another until you dry all that is in the body, then treat the wounds that are caused by burns.
li cure dou trembler	treat the shivering
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When any person trembles from cold or nerves, or from quartan fever or other ailments, it is fitting that you make four or four cauteries on the spine of the back, one cautery between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cautery at the waist, and one on the stomach at the olive cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	and let it trembling, and hasten the recovery of the health of the cold illness.
des pustules puans	pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	At times apparent through the body bathed, or pus-filled blisters, that come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	then it is fitting at the first when they appear that you make a cautery on each head of the pustule.
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery of myrtle wood, the tip being set on fire, or of long aristole root, or with a lentil-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes the cauterization one begins when they appear, according to this manner, and they do not permit growth of tumors in front, but the excesses from which they come are broken off, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut.
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great losses of blood from the artery which is cut by the wound or in the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is most foul to smell.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And in any case, when this happens to anyone, hasten to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it tightly until the bleeding stops beneath your finger, and no more blood flows.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then heat the olive cauteries, both small and large, until they are entirely red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then apply it, whether large or small according to the wound and the limb in which the artery runs, and place the cautery over that vein where you hold your hand, and keep the cautery there until the blood is coagulated.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it leaps out when you remove your finger from above the vein, and the cauteries are used, so take quickly another from the cauteries that are in the flame.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease to do this one after another until the blood is coagulated;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood flows from the artery, one cannot coagulate it well by itself when the artery is large, unless it is by one of the four methods that we have said:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by fire cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by strong tying with thread, or by medicines placed on which have the power to draw out blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and may be tied and held at the onset.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will treat the stench from lime closely with cloths or put burning things there, or other similar things, if it does not help much, then it should be discontinued.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they have neither mirror nor medicine present, they should place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and extend it well so that it is drawn out above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the thread, but moisten it often with cold dew that it may be very cold until the blood is frozen and collected and drawn out;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make incisions in front of the parts that require cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book on wound treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter where it is fitting to use the fire cautery or the cautery of burning medicines, and the blisters and their causes and the instruments and the forms of the cauteries;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have set out this chapter from the hand to the foot, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same way as one finds it more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And since I begin this, it is necessary, dear friend, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first on the cauteries, and for this reason it is necessary greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	or there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you that you undertake no folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if coming from those who are so affected by their illness that they die slightly due to the fear they find in their illness, and because of the severity of their malady;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of these, some give their sense and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is sudden.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting that you consent to those who come to you and have this manner, but put more careful consideration in your honor than in your greed, and do not readily give of what you are uncertain, but only of what you can take and lose;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use pronouncement and indication in the treatment of your patients for their health to be converted;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and he will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear friend, Our Lord gives you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to breathe in the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have instructed this chapter by discussing it section by section, as I did in the chapter on fire cauteries, where I spoke of the head down to the feet, because you will find it more easily comprehensible.
dou chief plein d’aigue	of the head full of fluid
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease comes very often to children at birth, and when the birthing hands hold too tightly the head of the child.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from a cause that we do not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease occur in anyone other than children, and among those I have seen, many died quickly.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And because of this, it seems to me that I should leave the work in partial treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw the child whose shoulder was full of fluid, and the head was growing larger each day to the point it could no longer support it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture was so great that it caused death, and this moisture is gathered around the bone above the scaphoid, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the operations must be such that if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you make a wide incision through the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two of our fingers, so that the moisture can drain.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see the form of the spatumile:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is greater, and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and the signs that you see at the corners of the shoulder for each part, and the sharp pain when you press it from within with your hand, this does not concern you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	it is necessary that you make three cuts in the shoulder in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture out.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After dressing the cuts with cloths and powders, and applying wine and oil, leave it thus for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then release it, and treat the wound with tents and ointments, and let the shoulder strengthen gradually. Then give the patient dry meat with a little moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incising is that you look for where the abscess is largest, and the collection of pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for it never occurs before;
aucune fois derrier;	no time behind;
aucune fois en destre;	no time on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and no time on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut accordingly where the abscess is largest, and where the collection of pus is, making the incision according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be sure not to cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and let the blood flow freely, so that the patient heals through the discharge of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "catarre" in the eyes or the testicles, and the disease is ancient, and medical treatment does not help much, then the last remedy is the cautery with that of which one will cauterize the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you are to see the patient, the sick person must turn their head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the area with an abrasive cloth until the arteries are visible, then remove the sick person's collar completely;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein is located, and the ears are behind both sides, and they are slightly raised;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the edges with ink, then incise both sides with a sharp spatulum in two parts, until the vein is cut to the bone, and this should be done on the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, place the spatule over the artery and cut above it, cutting as much as twice through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let the blood flow out continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open with pressure, then measure the quantity of three doux, mark with ink, and cut until the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and what must be let out of the blood is 6 quarts, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone point of syphilis, and the abscess does not come to a head, then incise the wound and apply a dressing, and treat with ointment until it heals.
de emigrainne	Of emigrainne
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient emigrainne comes, and acute cataract, due to the moistures of tears and the heats in the temples and old, ancient fever and similar things, and it is treated with methods of medicinal treatments and all such means do not benefit it, then extract the arteries in the temples and use cautery, as we have recounted.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method for extracting them is that the patient should pull from the hairs of his temples, and feel for the artery that appears in the temple, for it appears well by its pulsation, and is little displaced in some people who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is bound, draw the patient's neck with some cloths, then rub the back with a rough cloth, and wash the back with hot water until the arteries appear clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula of copper that is in the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then cauterize the skin lightly until you see the artery, then draw it up with forceps, and pull away all the threads that are beneath each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, turn it with the point of the bisturi, then cut that part according to the size of the two shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, neither will the stone pass completely through.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	and draw blood from six parts, until three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you must tie it with two strong threads of silk, that putrefaction not arise before the suddenness of the wound, and prevent hemorrhage.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut the excess skin between the two threads in that same hour, and then, if you see fit, apply the cautery of the surgical cautery to the bone until the shoulder is severed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and this is the main work, if the patient has no fever and he is of warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cauteries are help to finish the moistures:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for it is of greater help in finishing the moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or it is necessary for the extraction of arteries to fill the cavity with old cotton and place something well-made over it;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are removed, it should be treated with dry medicinal substances that promote healing, and with bandages until it is healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if there is no cord from the artery as much as you work, then hasten to cauterize with fire, or fill the cavity with vitriol and squeeze it with your hand so that it dries up;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have this at hand, place on the cavity your finger so that it dries, and remove the cotton with cold water until it is saturated, and hold it steady as it should be;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and he who is more weakened and lighter in the extraction of the artery, you should cauterize the vein of this cutting cautery in two parts, but the cutting edges be well thick to hold longer their heat.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too cold, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should have between the two knives a thickness of good space, and when you have joined the two ends, then place the hot iron on it until it comes just to the bone, and cut the vein in two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and let them be spaced apart between the two heads because they are not joined together by this cautery from end to end.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes are flowing down the veins that are on the side of the head, and medical treatment does not help, and you see the patient's face turn red, and feel tremors on the forehead as if from shivering.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and when they are held and moist so that the hairs of the papers fall out, and the papers become heated, and scalded by the heat of the tears, it needs this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "bruised wound treatment," and you should do this for a patient who has this illness: have them lie on their back and mark the hairs they have or on their forehead, then make three equal divisions or grooves on the forehead according to its length.
