aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after suturing, then clip the head of the shoulder that appears with threads, until there are only four threads remaining;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then arrange them one over the other in the shape of a cross, and bind the fat, which we have said is below the skin of the hips, with a strong bandage of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then envelop the head of the shoulder with cloth, and bind it tightly in two places, so that no fluid that nourishes it can enter into it, and an abscess does not arise;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and again put the bandage according to the first long bandage around it, and after these two bandages leave a space under the heart of the shoulder blade as large as one hand;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and afterwards the rest according to the roundness that the egg carried;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then place in the part that is under the skin of the shoulder blade, as much as the wound requires, and the bow, as we have said above;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply moistened wool in oil, and place it on the wounds, and put the bandage as we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the whites of the eyes are cauterized to prevent bleeding after incision due to doubt.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the ligature until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in falling off, then dissolve it with hot water, and apply what we have said until it falls off.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with other dressings until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this case, I have never known anyone to dare treat it with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like the branches intertwined around a vine, in such a manner that you bind the vessels, after cutting them lightly during dislocation.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then take some of it, and treat the abscess of those who work until the vessels clot.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the treatment as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	No occasion comes of rupture in veins, as we have said, and open the eyes;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and feel no parts of the intestines at the incisions, and if any are felt, it is little, and change all hours.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and in any case, if it remains too long in this spot, the wound or syphilis will develop, as parts of the intestines are felt.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the extension of syphilis which is in the veins, as we have said, because it extends, then softens and swells the eyes and opens.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment involves fire cautery, as we have already said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with a iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the patient lies sovin on his back between your hands, then cover the part of the rupture swollen in width according to the size of three doix.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the syface that is under the skin where it protrudes, then take the rag and place it over the apparent part of the syface.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it well on the abdomen, then suture the two apparent parts of the syface over the rag, and suture them both.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the wart, and do not cut or extend the egg nor anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the branch of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it as you would treat wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, cleanse and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The seam is constrained, and shows no sign in the rupture, and the cauteries are healed in this place, and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the cheeks
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the soles of the feet become softened in some people because the flesh within is softened, and it must be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, to make the patient lie on their back, and cut away the softened skin above the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then join the two edges with a缝合线，如果你愿意，可以将多余的软化皮肤用三针或四针牢固地缝合。请注意，这里的"costure"在古法语中意为缝合线或缝合针。
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then stitch between the seams, and treat the wound like other wounds until it heals, and change the bandage.
dou chastrement	by just punishment
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Castrations are forbidden in our law, and because of this, I shall not speak of them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary to use force only for two manners:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	of which one is that the eyes should be able to answer when asked and know how to treat the wound;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate some animals to help us, such as goats, sheep, and dogs, and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I therefore say that castration is performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction, or by splitting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one we perform by attraction, place the animal in hot water until the cords are softened and remain;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them with your hand, until they are relaxed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castration of the tail:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary to hold the animal, and press the skin of the cords with your left hand, then tie the suspender, and cut each testicle cleanly when you have well scalded them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and he lets any little pus and thin pus which is under the vessels remain.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that done by attraction, for in attraction, by chance, some of the testicles remain, causing the beast to desire lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Herms and Hermaphrodites are according to two methods in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two testicles, it is open as if it were the shape of a woman's figure, or it has hair, and sometimes in the course of urination.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women, placed above the knife as a rod and two coins.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for men and women is that you clean all the wounds thoroughly, and treat them as other wounds.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, of men whose urine jumps through the skin of the scrotum, it has no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the beard
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentingene is an adjointed char on the natural part, as it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is its treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you dye the excess of the tentingene with your hand or fingers, and apply it lightly.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not use too strong a fomentation, lest blood flow occur, and continue the treatment until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and for another char that arises at the opening of the arm, apply it, and sometimes jump out forcefully, and resembles a cow, and because of this they called it in ancient times "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must cut it, as we have said regarding the tumor and its treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic if it is when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the wound is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and is natured at birth, or accident by disease that has come.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by sharp injury, or through a fine or thick thread, and is made in the flesh, or in the sides, or beneath, or that be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and defend conception, childbirth, and by accident the flowers to have.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is through the gaze of the midwife.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swellings are near and apparent, seek with your fingers or touch them.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is through a fine thread, and it is near the two lips, hasten, and remove it thus.
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and have the woman on her back, spreading her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then spread the two lips until the underlying flesh is round and over the stoppers;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and fat in oil, and place it over the wound, and let the woman lie on her back each day so that it does not heal too quickly.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilis is hard and thick, it is necessary to scrape with a spatula resembling a bay leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the stoppers are of born flesh, suspend them at the inch and the gill;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and use the blood-stanching medicines, such as ice, dragon's blood, incense, and abundant egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then administer a broad pledget of wick, so that the wound cannot heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus be long, and administer a tent of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue to treat with other remedies until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when a carbuncle brings forth pus, it should be treated according to this method, unless it is an encrusted abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an encrusted abscess in the carbuncle, one should not touch it to incise.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that without cause commonly occur, and when hemorrhoids are old they become tumors.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have already described the symptoms of aus, and the signs, and I will now say those that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and thrombosed ones, when they are fully ripe in the carbuncle, do not appear by touch; except those cured with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the sore, which one can feel, are those one can treat.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you should place the woman in a cold room, then warm the altar with tongs, and put the copa in its roots, then sprinkle with medicines that constrict blood, such as açaí, dragon's blood, and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then let his feet rest against the wall for an hour, then place them in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if the bleeding continues, have him sit in a decoction of sumac and bark of pomegranate peels and galls and similar things, then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and apply it as a poultice to his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops bleeding, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply suction cups to the back and breasts without causing injury;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, and mix it with the juice of plantain or agrimony with old wine, and apply it to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has come to a head, treat the place with ointment until it heals.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles a rough head, so it should be treated as I have said for the thumb.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue the treatment until he is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses of the arm
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the arm, such as chancre, porous abscess, herpes, estiomenes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must speak in this treatise of the hot abscess that comes from the arsis, which is not one of the abscesses that boil over.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the iron work, observe whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore, do not hasten to pierce it; let it continue to mature until the pain is alleviated.
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then place the patient on a seat, and have two small seats where he can recline, and support him on his back and align his feet with the lower part of the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and spread his thighs apart, and place his arms over his knees, and bind them well with a firm band.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then apply the cautery to the right side, and bring the instrument used for opening the mouth of the blister hereafter described.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and you must ensure that when you see the instrument administered to this blister, you insert the first needle to know the depth of the blister, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not burn the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instruments are larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with strips of cloth, so that the instruments do not cause pain.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he place the horn of the instrument above, and hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess is open, and it is made soft by hand, it is necessary to cover it with a cloth, or a sponge soaked in liquid.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is evacuated, it is necessary that you place wet cloths in oil of rosemary, or in oil of turpentine.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth over the depth of the wound, and put above the wound and on the blade clean wet cloths in water or cooked oil.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply the treatment after two days of ointment application until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and occasionally lift the wound and the sore with a clyster of water and honey, and then with water or roots of lily and wormwood that have been cooked.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then resume the ointment application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is placed on the margin, you must take care to avoid cauterizing with iron, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the natural birth figures, and the signs are when you see the woman press her abdomen, and desire to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then hasten for the child to be born quickly.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then know that this birth is according to the natural figure, and the child comes out with its head, and the next one follows with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his abdomen, so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends on its head, she follows with him, and the mature ones are cleansed of their superfluities by good cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and he who comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	for he comes sometimes on his feet, and comes forth into the body or the shoulder, and the hands, or where he comes on the abdomen, or side, and is turned by accident over the neck, and in other evil shapes.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary that the midwife be wise and subtle in these matters, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes how one should assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If a child comes to his head through natural birth, and the mother gives birth easily, and the virtue of her is weak, then I make her sit on a saddle, or the women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and arise her nature of oil or fenugreek that is cooked, and then pour the bile between her two small spatulas as their form is.
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut the second one, and scrape with her nail until the moisture that is contained comes out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the abdomen of the woman until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must cleanse the woman with fenugreek seed oil and olive oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	and then make her breathe deeply and expel air forcefully, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if now treat the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands swell, you must reset them gently little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, you place the woman on the seat and lift her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then place the seat on the ground, and hold the woman so she does not move during the procedure;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot enter and the child has died, you cut the hand with the knife that was placed before, and extract the child, resetting it equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	from the issue of the child at his feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	and if the child comes to its feet, you must lift them up;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then file little by little, until they are equal;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then pinch the flesh and stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	Can it jump up to the knees if commanded, and make it sneeze by pressing.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps, if God wills it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not feverish as we have said, turn it little by little, until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is lightly.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come to pass as we have, say take a piece of flax thread, and silk oil, and melted gum, and grind them all in the mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply the nature of the woman inside and over this ointment, then make her sit in warm water until below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is softened underneath, he makes a collar of myrrh, puts it there, and lets it remain one hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then he makes it sit on the seat, then he makes it sneeze and holds its mouth and nose, and he gently rubs its belly, for the child jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the issue from the child above his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes into this form, place his hands little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then it is suspended around its neck, and its feet hang down, and it lies on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold its hands little by little, and then place its hands on the belly, and remove the cushions underneath, until it is ready to hang down.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not come out, take its feet and twist them, then twist its head upward, and push with your hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and slowly the child comes out;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to strain herself until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the issue of the child which comes with one hand wide open
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	it is necessary to devise ways to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be brought back, lift the woman and go;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, make her lie on the bed, and twist her legs;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the muscillaige as I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, place her on the seat, then try to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and if the child is in its natural position, make her sneeze, and instruct her to bear with it until the child passes.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the birth of the child at its neck, and have spread its hands, and its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the bail hold her hand, then turn it little by little, and she gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is equal, place the natural muscular texture of flax and oil on it, as we have said, then instruct her to move it little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, place her on the seat, and instruct her to bear with it;
et la fai esternuer.	and make them sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in this same manner for all the secondine
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to force in this manner on the second joint, empty the second joint with your finger, until all the moisture is removed;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the injury can be made on its face and on its neck, then empty it from the mouth, do not hold it back, and suffocate the injury;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child back in, until you have placed it as it should be, and instruct the woman to push once.
adonques si istra legierement.	then gently insert it.
de l’issue des gemelz	from the issue of the twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born often, and sometimes three or four are born.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and rarely happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and do not live, if at all;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know these, that they are multiplied, and are severed by the syphilitic who devises them, who is attached to the mouth;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they issue naturally like ten under one, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they issue smoothly, the treatment as we have said, and let the fine cloth do quickly and easily what it does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it is worth to bring about healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the liver I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, and are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the glorious sage, and it is fitting that the bailiff know all this, for by accident such things happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	it should be done according to what is fitting.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman who has died with a stillborn child or is pregnant, as I have said in the division, and there is no discharge, and you are forced to perform manual procedures;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	it is fitting that you know whether the woman is in good health, and has no complications or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	if it is necessary to treat the woman on her back, and let her shoulders inclined downward, and the legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and let the minister place her in two parts, or bind her to the bed so that she is not treated when the child descends;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the patient with moist oils mixed with myrtle and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and spices.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then gently place them on the patient, then choose a location where she will lie that is suitable for this, and ensure that the child is prepared to descend onto her head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the lancet is inserted into his eyes or neck or in his mouth or under the palate or below the beard or in the temple or near the ribs, and if the descent is on a vein, then the lancet or knife and middle ribs are pierced;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that you hold the lancet in your right hand, and place the clamp between the fingers of your left hand, and gently press with all your hand, and insert the lancet into any of these places that we have mentioned, until it comes to the thing empty.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of the lancet:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert it against the other lancet, or the third if you need it, so that the extractions be equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then let it be equal in moving from one side to the other, to allow it to come out, and may the teeth be used to hold it, as is shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part of it remains, instruct the patient to move any of his eye muscles, and direct them to that part, and cut the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains none of it, place this tooth or something higher on the area, and do so until all of it is out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be brought back due to contraction, then you must wrap it with a cloth, until all of it comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then on the joint of the sole or with the knife, and so you must do in the other hand, and with both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the child is large and the birth canal is narrow, or there is an acute swelling gathered, you must insert the pointed spatule between your hands, cut the swelling, and extract the acute swelling;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you may do it with the instrument called "almidach", whose form comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and do the same if the infant has a large head naturally.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then cut the bones with the tongs, and if the head has come out and is held by the forceps, split it until the moisture that is more inside comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it out in pieces as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the abdomen or beneath the ribs, you must puncture it until the fluids flow.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is under its feet, the traction is light, and the direction to the mouth of the birth canal is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is swollen in the abdomen or the testicles, you must extract it with a knife wrapped in a cloth.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut open the abdomen or the testicles until the fluids that are inside flow out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is amputated and the head remains, pour hot oil on its hand to burn it, and cut it down to the opening of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then one to two drops of wine or vinegar;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the opening of the boil is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has come about, it should not be worked on, but rather moist and greasy substances should be applied.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply plasters, and soak a cloth in moistening and softening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the injury is on his side, and you can set it equal, apply what we have said for a living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if we do not have the ability, apply wine in small amounts, and do not leave any of the vinegar behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, administer to them what we have said for abscesses that come in the liver;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, it should be treated with cold water, and other dressings should be administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly an infant had died, then I sutured the other [one] over it, and prevented the death of the other.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess formed in the mouth, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the treatment, and I thought long about it, and could not staunch the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster with strong吸引力，从中取出了一块骨头，之后几天又取出了其他一些。
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvelled much, for the belly has no bone.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I wish the wound clean, and in my hands bones, until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and I kept the woman long thus, and it was indeed a little bone from the shoulder.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter only because when the master finds an unusual thing, he should know how to provide aid.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to reset the dislocation to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	After this comes the form of the presser, to which one applies the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns of the head of the two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	All in all, the horns should be more delicate of the retractor, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth be twice as wide, and the margin of the branches one palm and a half long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs there should be two adjustments of the same wood, which should be firmly fixed in both, half a palm long or a bit more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two adjustments are inserted in the mouth of the clamp to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, resembling it more subtle and lighter, be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the likeness of tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and let it have two shoulder joints, as you see, of long width, and two bones of breadth;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the vein open for the entire instrument, place the woman on the bed, with her feet hanging and legs spread, then insert the two shoulder joints of the instrument together into the vein, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then manipulate the instrument with your hand as you would with tongs, equally on both sides, according to the quantity that you see needs to open the mouth of the vein, so that it does what it should.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This instrument is entirely above ground, and its images are multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the mirrors have been prepared, they are more haste in their work, and appear taller to them by virtue of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not use the instrument properly unless it is prepared, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the secondine is retained in childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her hips, and then make her sneeze by sniffing condisi, and hold her hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she jumps because of this, well done.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	And if she does not jump, take a pot, and make a perforation or coverleap, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the mare, such as caraway, rue, fennel, chamomile, cassia, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or any of them, be cooked or boiled in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put a cane or pertus in the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the maris, until the vapors enter the maris;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make him sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second joint moves quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment, and is not cured, command the bailiff to moisten his left hand in sesame oil or in tallow grease, and then apply it to the affected area, and seek a second opinion.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take it out and extend it little by little straight, so that the maris does not cry at the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it must be moved lightly to the right and to the left, and then treat;
si venra et se desaerdra.	if it comes and is reduced.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the nostril is narrowed, we have said the treatment for sneezing and fumigating herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not of all that we have said, take care that you do not err in treating.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it must be that which is at the opening of the nostril, that you bind it to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse with an ointment enema.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if it heals and returns, and will come forth.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nonetheless, when she [it] produces such a bad smell in the stomach and head, and causes the patient discomfort.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then one must therefore perform appropriate fumigations for it:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	none of the ancients have proven the fumigation with cress and dried figs effective.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for the retention of flowers and the secondine is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it appears similar to a cane, and one places the head subtlety in its nature, and the shoulders wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigations be above the coals, and the scab until it is weakened, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the fundament pierced, but instead have it stopped by some subtle means.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it is necessary for the lady to pierce this side according to her duty, and she does not pierce it with a sharp spatillum, and be careful that the insertion does not touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place on moistened wool in wine and oil, and apply the ointment treatment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not close, put or hold a plug of lint, and let it remain in place, and be removed when the child seems ready to go into chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this塞封 comes suddenly from a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	then it is necessary to cauterize it suddenly:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it needs to be treated, as we have said for the lead plunger.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from the fundament are nodations, and grow larger as they leave the fundament, or in the space between two parts, for one fistula or many.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that node is old, you operate, and cure moist white or fine warts, and sometimes these Persian fistulas.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are known by those who experience excretion or windiness when the patient has an excretion, and by accident due to a sudden movement.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if the fistulas extend as far as the bladder, and as far as the midpoint of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they reach as far as the hip joint, and as far as the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the Persian fistula in the anus, and not elsewhere:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you place your index finger or foundation, and insert a thin needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if there is tortuosity, insert a thin catheter of linen, or horsehair, as long as you feel the catheter or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or wind or pus, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	you know that it does not perforate;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to treat.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is pierced to the bladder or to the urethra, it will discharge urine, and cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	if it perforates to the hip joint, the catheter comes from that place.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no torsion and the source of the pain is within, it is set in place by itself, and neither medicine nor sudden application of ointment helps.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in Persian fistulas there is no cure other than labor and the vain effort of foolish people who undertake it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	For those that are neither Persian nor ancient, there is hope of healing with iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies on his back.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient stretches his legs up to his thighs, and bends his knees toward his abdomen.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then apply a bandage of linen or wool if there is torsion, as long as you know where the bandage should be applied.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels pain deep within the pelvis, you must place your index finger there; if then you sense that the nerves have been punctured;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and if you discover that it is the sac or flesh between your finger and thumb, then you know it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if there is no travail there, it cannot be cured.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can cure well some, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the aid that one makes, it is that one heats the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and he heats it thoroughly in the fistula until it comes from the pelvis.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that these charred cinders have been burned, which resemble the feathers of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then dress the wet wounds with butter until the cinders are out, then dress with ointment to heal the flesh and join it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus set, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this, cannot be cured otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent is inserted, and does not pierce to the depth which is the foundation, and between your finger and the tent place a thick covering of flesh or grease, and you will see the fistula where the covering is removed.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the pus from the beginning of the fistula, and apply it before the tent, and cauterize after, until it reaches the head of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be released, and fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and remove those charred marks that seem like a bird's feather, and let none remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the seton fails and cuts between you and the wound, cauterize with fire or medicinal water.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these charred areas, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	and the treatment of wet tents with butter or ground cheese, until the wounds emit pus, and then let the charred areas burn in the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	and treat the wound with tight ointments containing hard charcoal, and these are the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is sound and does not return again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes just to the point of the fundament and is distant from the body, touch or place your finger at the fundament, and inquire it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent and between them is linen or silk or flesh, or it is about to pierce, do not have any outlets unless there is a way of faith and hope, through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cautery it as we have said, or you cauterize it through and through, or if you can, put in tents and dressings as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not apply too much powder, so that you do not cauterize the tissue that holds the foundation, and let the excretions come through it without willing it;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then dress the wound as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance it will be healed, or you remove that covering and cleanse it since it is cauterized from the foundation, or with a tent or another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cleanse the wounded flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then study to restore the wound, and to stop the fistula below the fundament:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter matter for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert a probe into the fistula, and it is situated near the fundament beneath the skin, take a probe pierced at the end according to this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And you poke the thread into two turns, and push the tent onto all the thread in the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	and if it is deep within the margin of the fundament, then extract the thread of that puncture, as you would insert your finger or probe.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and join the two heads together, hold them against each other, and let them one day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold them together once, until the thread covers the spaces between the two, and sews.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is stitched and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not perforate, make it perforate in all ways that you can, provided it is not too close to the surface.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not fitting to cauterize for the ligature if too close to the surface, and then treat, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous spur from which we make the fistula is very acute and sharp.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand, no, because what should not be covered is not to be sewn, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Abscesses are according to two methods:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	or they are within the foundation, as grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and inside it is blood, and there are one or more, and they protrude from the foundation and at the head of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that protrude have little moisture, and inside are a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them within the foundation, is that you instruct the patient to sweat in order to release into rooms, until the foundation comes forth, and the threads appear;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you are in a hurry, and it can be held with tongs, or you hold it with your fingernail, then pull it by its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the censer cannot hold them due to moisture, they take it by the cord, or with cotton, or a piece of camlet;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them with both hands, then copes them, and sprinkle over them some warm powders that are used for the fire cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as described in the chapter on cauterization, and treat them with other dressings until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, you cauterize the patient with a caustic cloth to wash away what is at the foundation, so that it may come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	and if the patient presents symptoms, and if the threads are broken at the foundation, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grasp them with your finger or tongs, cut them off, then treat and clean them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you administer the suturing according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take a thread of cloth, and put it through a needle, and then draw the thread over and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and so be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and hold the thread tight, then tie the thread, and withdraw the needle, and do so with all the others, leaving one to drain the excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a pad of woolen cloth in oil of rose or ointment, and place it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let it be until it heals, and when they have healed, give them ointment and other treatment until he is cured.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of dry the wound or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there is a sudden drying up of bile in the intestines, and by constraint of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	Then you must reset at the end of a splinter or under your nail the bark above, which you leave to dry.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	and cure it until it is healed as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then resume the scraping more forcefully than before, until it heals and is scorched.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until he is healed.
dou fremit	of trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A formice is a small deceitful appearance on the body, and goes very quickly.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the truth is found when it is touched, and one feels it like a death tremor, spreading throughout the body, more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from an ostrich feather, or a very strong eagle feather, and place the quill on the tremor, so that the red circle completely encircles the tremor.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand around the quill so that you cover the tremor completely, and apply it well, rooting out the tremor from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do it with a needle of spider silk or iron according to this form, and make it thin underneath and drawing on top:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	ne mie perciet, pour mieux tenir au doigt, et mouvoir presser.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, cauterize the fremit, as it is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the shoulder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes one makes a blister with silver or mercury, or melted lead or mesh;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes one makes these instruments small and large, according to those to whom they are applied.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those that are used in the treatment of children and who are weak and in pain, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the shoulder, whether small or large, is such that the breasts are tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there be a deviation or the stomach be tied, as you see, and the head be pierced within;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and have two perforations on one side, and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and let the wounds where one places the medicines from an animal bladder or parchment be pierced entirely with small perforations, and there should be a thumb's breadth between each perforation, then pour in these perforations strong thread twisted into ten or more parts, and join the wound as one would a sheep.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, seal it with a strong thread at the opening of the instrument, then cauterize;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	and let the medicine neither be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or yolk of egg, or something similar, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the minister draws it with both hands until it is completely full, then removes the clyster, and lifts the patient's legs against the wall, and if the medicine seems to come out, he lets the patient urinate as much as he can.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if it sleeps all night, it is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you clysterize for a disease of bowel discharge, and the medicine hastens to come out, then repeat it as much as he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	and if the hemorrhoid is external or internal, or abscess, let the clyster be as subtle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle clyster with which the skin is compressed:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already said in the division of treating wounds:
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will say of the treatments of hands and medicine, according to the accomplishment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the joints or parts where they are made, and of what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by the impact of a stone, and cutting with a sword or knife, or a lance or staff or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or by those made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the thigh, or the belly, or the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, take care if it is by the impact of a stone or similar things, and the skin is always torn and the wound large, and you slightly suspect an abscess.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	if you find the head of the shoulder soonest in need of healing when little blood comes from the wound, and let it be healed on the contrary side of the broken part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and choose the patient who is full of wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	and if he does not wish to be healed, let his flesh be reduced, and do not let him drink wine or eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place on the wound, if abscesses form and come to a head, only moistened cotton in rose oil, or in styptic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no warm abscess, place on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and has not dried by the air, powder, which I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the physician has bled it, he should apply some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like a sword cut and similar ones, and the edges cannot be brought together by stretching, sew them together, as I will say for wounds of the belly, concerning stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to bone and is unstable, holding only by a little, then bind it;
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	then treat the wound with medicine, and restore firm flesh instead of skin, and instruct the patient to eat solid meats, such as heads and cooked wheat, like poultry, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rotten skin and it does not affect the bone, then cover the rot entirely, apply powder, and then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if it has an artery in the wound or vein, which bleeds profusely, and cannot be stopped by medicines, then ligature the artery, and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
