et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and have another minister extend his hand above in such a manner that he places his hands under the armpits, then bind it with a cloth around the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another hold the head of the patient.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and extend upwards and downwards at once, so that the patient is lifted from the ground at once, and remains suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for the four similarities, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then it must be treated for its likeness.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When dislocation is at the shoulder blade, you must stabilize the patient on the healthy side, then place the ligament at the root of the thigh, and below the angle, then tie it above towards the angle and away from the spine.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then bind the other minister's arm, and embrace the large ligament of the injured thigh, and extend it downward firmly.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	it will now return to its place.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is less severe than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot tighten it in this manner as we have said, then you must tie the patient's two feet together with a strong ligature above the ankles and knees, and ensure that the injured leg is extended about two fingers' breadth more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then let it hang from the head of a stake, and two arms length.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then command the minister to embrace the head of the thigh, and let others hang with the patient who embraces firmly the thigh, for the joint returns quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is downward, the patient lies down, as we have said in that concerning gilbositeit, and draw the ligament on the injured leg properly, and on the heel also.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two hot coals, one on the head and the other on the heel, then insert the coal between the thighs of the patient in the proper position.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and plant dry cloths between, so that it does not blister the patient, then stretch each minister before him, and align the eyes with his hand at the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	And if it returns, that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	And if not, place it on the table and press it as we have said in the gilbositeit, and let the patient lie on the good side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to stretch the injured leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and place the eyes where the pain is on the injured leg, then press with the other hand, and stretch downward toward the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And when the dislocation is behind, it is not necessary to stretch the injured part downward or lift it off the ground. Instead, it should be positioned as if the hip were dislocated behind, as we have said regarding the position on the two hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it should be above its surface, and the ligament stretched as we have said before, and must be pressed on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be in place when the patient extends his legs, and they will be equal;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then adjust the thighs, and apply the plaster, and bind it with a bandage, so that the hips do not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and let it rest for 3 or 4 days, then remove the bandage, and apply the plaster again;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are equal, bind it as before, and let it rest for 3 days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then release the ligature, and let it go freely until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	it is to say, within and without, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	and does not dislocate at the front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is this: you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if it does not fit against the thigh, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all this is that you instruct the patient to sit straight, and extend their leg if possible, and place your back against theirs, and put their foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take his knee with your palms, and draw it between your two hands, then bend the two sides of the knee apart;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and extend his foot further, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he moves his leg lightly with his thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the poultice, and keep the leg elevated at the thigh, and bind them tightly for three or four days, then release the binding.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not allow the patient to walk much until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not straight, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The ankle is sometimes injured, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign is that the ankle is swollen, and tends forward to the part where it is dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The treatment is light, and one should gently extend it with his hands when he is merely suspected.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated completely, you must seat the patient upright, and hold him by the ministers [slaves or attendants] except by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then draw the foot to you with your right hand, and then to the left twice, then extend it upward, and firmly place the foot upward;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice as we have said, by firmly placing and drawing the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, that is well;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if this does not work, restart the operation, for it returns;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return this way, place the patient on their back on the ground, and drive a stake firmly into the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around, so that the patient does not move.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then hold the thigh, and another minister extend the foot to the hand or the ligature, and tie it around the neck of the foot;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then extend each minister equally, and the stakes be placed firmly between the patient's thighs to hold the patient while extending.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then place the shoulder in an even position at its sides, and another minister hold the healthy leg from above, and the dislocation will quickly return to place.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is at the right point, put the plaster and plugs over it, stretch the skin, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are behind the ankle so that the bands are not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for 2 or 3 days, and as the bands soften, stretch them;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then release it on the third day or fourth, and instruct the patient not to move for 4 days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if it goes beyond this time, it is not certainty that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses arise, you must relieve them as we have said elsewhere until they are healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When they are dislocated, you must beautifully extend them with effort, and this is a light matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any notch of the foot or ankle, it is necessary to seat the patient on a firm surface or on a bench completely upright, and place his foot on what protrudes from these joints, then stretch his foot well until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when they are equal, and there is nothing apparent, put under the sole of the foot a shoulder blade for two shoulders, then hold it firmly, and leave it for three days, then release it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one sees it healing, many times the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not overly presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not wise in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not always patient and merciful and not too bold;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and use at the beginning of things to cool an abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, now reset the limb to its place, as the abscesses come to life.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is in place, administer things to appease the abscess with heat, and treat the wound as it should be, with drying ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and broken bones, set them, and do as we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and guard against entering a state of fear, as I have said, for it will affect you according to your Creator, and for the knowledge of your weapon and body.
